KHO DE BYAMS PA BLA MA SGRUB KHANG RIN PO CHE DE KHONG RE
GNYIS KYIS

YIN ZHUS PAR BRTEN KHA BTAGS DBANG LDAN ZHIG PHYAG NA

YOD PA DE SMON LAM GYIS MTSAMS SBYOR NAN TAN DU MDZAD NAS

RTEN DU BCUG STE SPYAN 'DREN GYI ZHU 'PHRIN PHUL BAS SBYIR

PA'I MTSAN CAN
